(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLICE NOTICES
I, R. Ramesh Kumar Natural, son of Thiru S. Ramalingam, residing at New No. 28/431, 18th Street, Korattur,
Chennai-600 080, By way of this Public Nitice, I inform that (late) Shri. C.M. Kannan, has legally adopted me as his son
on 8th January 2016 by way a Registered deed No. 9 of 2016, on the file of Sub-Registrar of Villivakkam, Chennai. My
adopted father Shri C.M. Kannan passed away on 14th February 2016, hereafter I shall be known as K. RAMESH KUMAR.
Chennai, 24th February 2016.

R. RAMESH KUMAR.
Adoptive son.

Hormones Changed for Women, has been certified by Dr. Saravana Valli Bose. By this, I May be treated as a female and
shall henceforth be known as RAJESHWARI.
